382→  bool cond2 = params.query.sym_size(-1) > 224 && is_dropout;\n   383→  if (input_requires_grad(params) && (is_sm86_or_sm89 || is_sm120_or_sm121) && (cond1 || cond2)) {\n   384→    if (debug) {\n   385→      TORCH_WARN(\n   386→          \"Flash attention currently doesn't support training with head_dim ∈ (192, 224] or \"\n   387→          \"(head_dim ∈ (224, 256] and dropout > 0.0) on gpu architectures in the range[sm86, sm89].\",\n   388→          \"Attempting to run with dropout set to: \", params.dropout,\n   389→          \"and head_dim: \",\n   390→          params.query.sym_size(-1), \" on a sm \", dprops->major, \".\",\n   391→          dprops->minor, \" gpu.\");\n   392→    }\n   393→    return false;\n   394→  }\n   395→  return true;\n   396→}\n   397→\n   398→bool check_flash_causal_non_square_seqlens(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   399→  // FlashAttention 2 updated the default mask meaning for causal in this PR:\n   400→  // 9e5e8bc91e it is now aligned to lower_right which would be a BC break\n   401→  // for non-square masks. We will not support non-square masks for causal w/ FAV2\n   402→  if (params.is_causal &&\n   403→      !params.query.is_nested() && !params.key.is_nested() &&\n   404→      params.query.sym_size(-2) != params.key.sym_size(-2)) {\n   405→    if (debug) {\n   406→      TORCH_WARN(\n   407→          \"Flash attention does not support the is_causal flag when seqlen_q != seqlen_k. \",\n   408→          \"Got seqlen_q: \", params.query.sym_size(-2), \" seqlen_k: \",\n   409→          params.key.sym_size(-2), \". If you would like to use causal attention with non-square masks, please see CausalAttnMask.\");\n   410→    }\n   411→    return false;\n   412→  }\n   413→  return true;\n   414→}\n   415→\n   416→bool check_all_tensors_on_device(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   417→  // Check that all tensors are on the GPU device\n   418→  // This should be handled by the stub dispatch, but we call can_use_*_attention\n   419→  // directly from python we need to ensure that the tensors are on cuda\n   420→  if (params.query.device().type() != at::DeviceType::CUDA) {\n   421→    if (debug) {\n   422→      TORCH_WARN(\n   423→          \"All tensors need to be on cuda device. Got query on device: \",\n   424→          params.query.device(),\n   425→          \", key on device: \",\n   426→          params.key.device(),\n   427→          \", value on device: \",\n   428→          params.value.device());\n   429→    }\n   430→    return false;\n   431→  }\n   432→  return true;\n   433→}\n   434→\n   435→bool check_cudnn_tensor_shapes(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   436→  const auto s_q = params.query.sym_size(2);\n   437→  const auto s_k = params.key.sym_size(2);\n   438→  const auto d_qk = params.query.sym_size(3);\n   439→  const auto d_v = params.value.sym_size(3);\n   440→  long cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();\n   441→  if (cudnn_version < 8903) {\n   442→    if (debug) {\n   443→      TORCH_WARN(\"SDPA fprop requires cudnn 8.9.3 or higher\");\n   444→    }\n   445→    return false;\n   446→  }\n   447→  if (cudnn_version < 8906 && params.dropout != 0.0) {\n   448→    if (debug) {\n   449→      TORCH_WARN(\"Dropout reference is only supported on 8.9.6 onwards.\");\n   450→    }\n   451→    return false;\n   452→  }\n   453→  auto head_dim_limit = 128;\n   454→  if (cudnn_version >= 91000) {\n   455→    auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n   456→    if (dprops->major == 9 && !dprops->minor) {\n   457→      head_dim_limit = 256;\n   458→    }\n   459→  }\n   460→  if (d_qk > head_dim_limit || d_v > head_dim_limit) {\n   461→    if (debug) {\n   462→      TORCH_WARN(\"head_dim should be no more than \", head_dim_limit);\n   463→    }\n   464→    return false;\n   465→  }\n   466→  if (d_qk % 8 != 0 || d_v % 8 != 0) {\n   467→    if (debug) {\n   468→      TORCH_WARN(\"head_dim should be a multiple of 8\");\n   469→    }\n   470→    return false;\n   471→  }\n   472→  if (cudnn_version < 8906 && s_k % 64 != 0 ) {\n   473→    if (debug) {\n   474→      TORCH_WARN(\"not-multiple-of-64 seq_kv is not supported below 8.9.6\");\n   475→    }\n   476→    return false;\n   477→  }\n   478→  if (cudnn_version < 90000) {\n   479→    if (s_q < 64) {\n   480→      if (debug) {\n   481→        TORCH_WARN(\"s_q less than 64 is not supported before cudnn 9.0.0\");\n   482→      }\n   483→      return false;\n   484→    }\n   485→    if (params.dropout != 0.0 && (s_q % 64 != 0 || s_k % 64 != 0)) {\n   486→      if (debug) {\n   487→        TORCH_WARN(\n   488→            \"s_q not a multiple of 64 with padding/dropout is not supported with cudnn version 9.0.0\");\n   489→      }\n   490→      return false;\n   491→    }\n   492→  }\n   493→  if (s_k == 1) {\n   494→    if (debug) {\n   495→      TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"cudnn SDPA does not support key/value sequence length 1.\");\n   496→    }\n   497→    return false;\n   498→  }\n   499→  if (s_q == 1 && params.dropout != 0.0) {\n   500→    if (debug) {\n   501→      TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"cudnn SDPA does not support query sequence length 1 with dropout.\");\n   502→    }\n   503→    return false;\n   504→  }\n   505→  return true;\n   506→}\n   507→\n   508→bool check_cudnn_layout(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   509→  const int64_t h = params.query.size(1);\n   510→  const int64_t s_q = params.query.size(2);\n   511→  const int64_t d = params.query.size(3);\n   512→  const int64_t s_k = params.key.size(2);\n   513→  const int64_t s_v = params.value.size(2);\n   514→  // corresponds to cuDNN's \"packed QKV\" layout\n   515→  const bool packed_query_layout_ok = (params.query.stride(0) == s_q * 3 * h * d) &&\n   516→                                 (params.query.stride(1) == d) &&\n   517→                                 (params.query.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n   518→                                 (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n   519→  const bool packed_key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * 3 * h * d) &&\n   520→                               (params.key.stride(1) == d) &&\n   521→                               (params.key.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n   522→                               (params.key.stride(3) == 1);\n   523→  const bool packed_value_layout_ok = (params.value.stride(0) == s_v * 3 * h * d) &&\n   524→                                 (params.value.stride(1) == d) &&\n   525→                                 (params.value.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n   526→                                 (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n   527→\n   528→  const bool packed_layout_ok = packed_query_layout_ok && packed_key_layout_ok && packed_value_layout_ok;\n   529→\n   530→  const bool query_layout_ok = (params.query.stride(0) == s_q * h * d) &&\n   531→                               (params.query.stride(1) == d) &&\n   532→                               (params.query.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n   533→                               (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n   534→  const bool key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * h * d) &&\n   535→                              (params.key.stride(1) == d) &&\n   536→                              (params.key.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n   537→                              (params.key.stride(3) == 1);\n   538→  const bool value_layout_ok = (params.value.stride(0) == s_v * h * d) &&\n   539→                               (params.value.stride(1) == d) &&\n   540→                               (params.value.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n   541→                               (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n   542→\n   543→  const bool layout_ok = query_layout_ok && key_layout_ok && value_layout_ok;\n   544→\n   545→  if (!packed_value_layout_ok && !layout_ok) {\n   546→    if (debug) {\n   547→      if (!packed_layout_ok) {\n   548→        if (!packed_query_layout_ok) {\n   549→          TORCH_WARN(\"Query tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.query.strides());\n   550→        }\n   551→        if (!packed_key_layout_ok) {\n   552→          TORCH_WARN(\"Key tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.key.strides());\n   553→        }\n   554→        if (!packed_value_layout_ok) {\n   555→          TORCH_WARN(\"Value tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.value.strides());\n   556→        }\n   557→      }\n   558→      if (!layout_ok) {\n   559→        if (!query_layout_ok) {\n   560→          TORCH_WARN(\"Query tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.query.strides());\n   561→        }\n   562→        if (!key_layout_ok) {\n   563→          TORCH_WARN(\"Key tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.key.strides());\n   564→        }\n   565→        if (!value_layout_ok) {\n   566→          TORCH_WARN(\"Value tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.value.strides());\n   567→        }\n   568→      }\n   569→    }\n   570→    return false;\n   571→  }\n   572→  return true;\n   573→}\n   574→\n   575→bool check_cudnn_hardware_support(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   576→  using sm80 = SMVersion<8, 0>;\n   577→  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n   578→  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n   579→  if (!check_sm_version<sm80, sm121>(dprops)) {\n   580→    if (debug) {\n   581→      TORCH_WARN(\n   582→          \"cuDNN MHA only supports gpu architectures in the range [sm80, sm121]. Attempting to run on a sm \",\n   583→          dprops->major,\n   584→          \".\",\n   585→          dprops->minor,\n   586→          \" gpu.\");\n   587→    }\n   588→    return false;\n   589→  }\n   590→  return true;\n   591→}\n   592→\n   593→bool check_for_nested_inputs(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   594→  static const bool enable_cudnn_nested = c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_NESTED_TENSOR_ENABLED\") == true;\n   595→  if (has_for_nested_inputs(params) && !enable_cudnn_nested) {\n   596→    if (debug) {\n   597→ not support backward.\");\n   603→      return false;\n   604→    }\n   605→  }\n   606→\n   607→  const auto dprop = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n   608→  // Check that the input is nested\n   609→  if (!(dprop->major == 9 || dprop->major == 10) && has_for_nested_inputs(params)) {\n   610→    if (debug) {\n   611→      TORCH_WARN(\"cuDNN SDPA supports nested tensors on SM 9.0, SM check_tensor_dtype(params, default_dtypes, debug);\n   627→  }\n   628→}\n   629→\n   630→bool check_runtime_disabled_cudnn(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   631→  // We check the global     TORCH_WARN(\"cuDNN SDPA is not deterministic.\");\n   648→      }\n   649→      return false;\n   650→    }\n   651→  }\n   652→  return true;\n   653→}\n   654→\n   655→} // namespace\n   656→\n   657→bool can_use_cudnn_attention(const sdp_params& params, bool debug) {\n   658→#if defined(USE_ROCM) || !AT_CUDNN_ENABLED() || !defined(CUDNN_VERSION)\n   659→  if (debug) {\n   660→    TORCH_WARN(\"Torch was not compiled with cuDNN attention.\");\n   661→  }\n   662→  return false;\n   663→#endif\n   664→#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && CUDNN_VERSION < 90000\n   665→  if (debug) {\n   666→    TORCH_WARN(CUDNN_VERSION, \" cuDNN version too old to use cuDNN Attention (< v9.0.0)\");\n   667→  }\n   668→  return false;\n   669→#endif\n   670→#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION)\n   671→  static auto cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();\n   672→  if (params.dropout > 0.0 && cudnn_version > 91100 && cudnn_version < 91400) {\n   673→    if (debug) {\n   674→      TORCH_WARN(CUDNN_VERSION, \" cuDNN version does not support droppout in SDPA (9.11 - 9.13).\");\n   675→    }\n   676→    return false;\n   677→  }\n   678→#endif\n   679→  // Define gate functions that determine if a flash kernel can be ran\n   680→  // Replace with std::to_array when we migrate to c++20\n   681→  constexpr auto general_constraints =\n   682→      c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(\n   683→          check_runtime_disabled_cudnn,\n   684→          check_for_nested_inputs,\n   685→          check_all_tensors_on_device,\n   686→          check_tensor_shapes,\n   687→          check_cudnn_deterministic,\n   688→          check_dtypes_low_precision,\n   689→          check_attn_mask_shape,\n   690→          check_cudnn_hardware_support\n   691→          );\n   692→  for (auto& constraint : general_constraints) {\n   693→    if (!constraint(params, debug)) {\n   694→      return false;\n   695→    }\n   696→  }\n   697→  constexpr auto dense_constraints =\n   698→      c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(\n   699→      check_nonzero_sequence_lengths_dense,\n   700→      check_last_dim_stride_equals_1_dense<true /*ignore_singleton_dim=*/>,\n   701→      check_batch_size_and_num_heads_dense<true /*enable_gqa*/, false /*requires_same_num_heads*/>,\n   702→      check_cudnn_tensor_shapes\n   703→  );\n   704→\n   705→  if (has_only_dense_inputs(params)) {\n   706→    for (auto& constraint : dense_constraints) {\n   707→      if (!constraint(params, debug)) {\n   708→        return false;\n   709→      }\n   710→    }\n   711→  }\n   712→  return true;\n   713→}\n   714→\n   715→bool is_flash_attention_available() {\n   716→#ifdef USE_FLASH_ATTENTION\n   717→  return true;\n   718→#else\n   719→  return false;\n   720→#endif\n   721→}\n   722→\n   723→bool can_use_flash_attention(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   724→#ifndef USE_FLASH_ATTENTION\n   725→  if (debug) {\n   726→    TORCH_WARN(\"Torch was not compiled with flash attention.\");\n   727→  }\n   728→  return false;\n   729→#else // defined(USE_FLASH_ATTENTION)\n   730→  // Define gate functions that determine if a flash kernel can be ran\n   731→  // Replace with std::to_array when we migrate to c++20\n   732→  constexpr auto general_constraints = c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(\n   733→      check_runtime_disabled_flash,\n   734→      check_all_tensors_on_device,\n   735→      check_tensor_shapes,\n   736→ 775→bool can_use_mem_efficient_attention(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   776→#ifndef USE_MEM_EFF_ATTENTION\n   777→  TORCH_WARN_ONCE(!debug, \"Torch was not compiled with memory efficient attention.\");\n   778→  return false;\n   779→#endif\n   780→  // Constraints specific to mem efficient attention\n   781→  constexpr auto less_than_sm80_mem_efficient_dtypes =\n   782→      c10::array_of<at::ScalarType>(at::kHalf, at::kFloat);\n   783→#ifdef USE_ROCM\n   784→  constexpr auto aotriton_mem_efficient_dtypes =\n   785→      c10::array_of<at::ScalarType>(at::kHalf, 796→      check_all_tensors_on_device,\n   797→      check_mem_efficient_hardware_support,\n   798→      check_tensor_shapes,\n   799→#ifdef USE_ROCM\n   800→      check_head_dim_size_flash<true /* return false;\n   823→      }\n   824→    }\n   825→  }\n   826→  if (has_only_dense_inputs(params)) {\n   827→    constexpr auto dense_constraints = c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, check_batch_size_and_num_heads_dense<false /*supports_grouped_query_attention=*/>);\n   831→    for (auto& constraint : dense_constraints) {\n   832→      if (!constraint(params, debug)) {\n   833→        return false;\n   834→      }\n   835→    }\n   836→  }\n   837→\n   838→#ifdef USE_ROCM\n   839→  if (params.attn_mask.has_value()) {\n   840→    const auto q_dtype = params.query.dtype();\n   841→    const auto bias_dtype = params.attn_mask.value().dtype();\n   842→    if (bias_dtype != at::kBool && bias_dtype != q_dtype) {\n   843→      TORCH_WARN(\"Efficient attention on ROCM requires greater_than_or_equal_sm80_mem_efficient_dtypes, debug);\n   855→  }\n   856→#endif\n   857→  return check_tensor_dtype(params, less_than_sm80_mem_efficient_dtypes, debug);\n   858→}\n   859→\n   860→SDPBackend select_sdp_backend(sdp_params const& kernel_params) {\n   861→  // This function defines the priority order of the different sdp backends\n   862→  // 1. Flash Attention\n   863→  // 2. Mem Efficient Attention\n   864→  // 3. Aborting execution.\")\n   922→  return SDPBackend::error;\n   923→}\n   924→\n   925→bool check_for_seq_len_1_nested_tensor(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   926→  // When this function is called we are assured that the nt is dim==4\n   927→  if (!params.query.is_nested()) {\n   928→    return true;\n   929→  }\n   930→\n   931→  const auto nt_q_tensor_impl =\n   932→      at::native::get_nested_tensor_impl(params.query);\n   933→  const at::Tensor& sizes = nt_q_tensor_impl->get_nested_sizes();\n   934→  auto* sizes_ptr = sizes.data_ptr<int64_t>();\n   935→  const int64_t n_tensors = params.query.size(0);\n   936→  const int64_t size_tensor_stride = sizes.stride(0);\n   937→\n   938→  // This is being called inside sdp with shape [batch, heads, {seq_len}, dim]\n   939→  for (const auto i : c10::irange(n_tensors)) {\n   940→    if (sizes_ptr[(i * size_tensor_stride) + 1] <= 1) {\n   941→      if (debug) {\n   942→        TORCH_WARN(\n   943→            \"Packed projection for fused kernels does not support sequence_length <= 1\");\n   944→      }\n   945→      return false;\n   946→    }\n   947→  }\n   948→\n   949→  return true;\n   950→}\n   951→\n   952→} // namespace sdp\n   953→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. sequence length 1 with dropout.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_cudnn_layout(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  const int64_t h = params.query.size(1);\n  const int64_t s_q = params.query.size(2);\n  const int64_t d = params.query.size(3);\n  const int64_t s_k = params.key.size(2);\n  const int64_t s_v = params.value.size(2);\n  // corresponds to cuDNN's \"packed QKV\" layout\n  const bool packed_query_layout_ok = (params.query.stride(0) == s_q * 3 * h * d) &&\n                                 (params.query.stride(1) == d) &&\n                                 (params.query.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n                                 (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n  const bool packed_key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * 3 * h * d) &&\n                               (params.key.stride(1) == d) &&\n                               (params.key.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n                               (params.key.stride(3) == 1);\n (params.value.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n                                 (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n\n  const bool packed_layout_ok = packed_query_layout_ok && packed_key_layout_ok && (params.query.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n                               (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n  const bool key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * h * d) &&\n         (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n\n  const bool layout_ok = query_layout_ok && key_layout_ok && value_layout_ok;\n\n  if (!packed_value_layout_ok && !layout_ok) {\n    if (debug) {\n      if TORCH_WARN(\"Value tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.value.strides());\n        }\n      }\n      if (!layout_ok) {\n        if (!query_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Query tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.query.strides());\n        }\n        if (!key_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Key tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.key.strides());\n        }\n        if (!value_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Value tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.value.strides());\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_cudnn_hardware_support(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  using sm80 = SMVersion<8, 0>;\n  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n  if (!check_sm_version<sm80, sm121>(dprops)) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"cuDNN MHA only supports gpu architectures in the range [sm80, sm121]. Attempting to run on a sm \",\n          dprops->major,\n          \".\",\n          dprops->minor,\n          \" gpu.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_for_nested_inputs(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  static const bool enable_cudnn_nested = c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_NESTED_TENSOR_ENABLED\") == true;\n  if (has_for_nested_inputs(params) && !enable_cudnn_nested) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"Experimental cuDNN SDPA nested tensor support is not enabled.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  } else if 141→constexpr int output_batch_size_dim = 0;  // also grad_output\n   142→constexpr int output_channels_dim = 1;\n   143→constexpr int weight_output_channels_dim = 0;\n   144→constexpr int ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n   150→//\n   151→// Checking\n   152→//\n   153→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n   154→\n   155→// Used on pad, stride and dilation\n   156→static void check_args(CheckedFrom c, IntArrayRef args, size_t expected_size, const char* arg_name)\n   157→{\n   158→  TORCH_CHECK(args.size() <= expected_size,\n   159→           \"Too many \", arg_name, \" values (\", args.size(), \") supplied, expecting \",\n   160→           expected_size, \" (while checking arguments for \", c, \")\");\n   161→  TORCH_CHECK(args.size() >= expected_size,\n   162→           \"Not enough \", arg_name, \" values (\", args.size(), \") supplied, expecting \",\n   163→           expected_size, \" (while checking arguments for \", c, \")\");\n   164→\n   165→  auto num_negative_values = std::count_if(args.begin(), args.end(), [](int x){return x < 0;});\n   166→  if (num_negative_values > 0){\n   167→    std::stringstream ss;\n   168→    ss << arg_name << \" should be greater than zero but got (\";\n   169→    std::copy(args.begin(), args.end() - 1, std::ostream_iterator<int>(ss,\", \"));\n   170→    ss << args.back() <<  \")\" << \" (while checking arguments for \" << c << \")\";\n   171→    TORCH_CHECK(false, ss.str());\n   172→  }\n   173→}\n   174→\n   175→\n   176→// NOTE [ Convolution checks ]\n   177→//\n   178→// NB: For many call sites, it is not strictly necessary to check all of\n   179→// these relationships (for example, for forward convolution, we compute\n   180→// the size of output ourselves, so we don't actually need to check\n   181→// output.  However, writing a single function that does everything\n   182→// means we get to reuse it for both forwards and all backwards\n   183→// variants, even when the set of \"real\" inputs varies.  The magic of\n   184→// relational computing!\n   185→//\n   186→// (There is one downside, which is that it is slightly harder to write\n   187→// error messages which are able to distinguish between real inputs\n   188→// (which the user can change) and computed inputs (which the user can\n   189→// only indirectly affect).  It would be an interesting exercise to\n   190→// come up with a general framework to handle such situations.)\n   191→inline void convolution_shape_check(\n   192→    CheckedFrom c,\n   193→    const TensorGeometryArg& input, const TensorGeometryArg& weight, const TensorGeometryArg& output,\n   194→    IntArrayRef padding, IntArrayRef stride, IntArrayRef dilation, int64_t groups)\n   195→{\n   196→  check_args(c, padding, input->dim() - 2, \"padding\");\n   197→  check_args(c, stride, padding.size(), \"stride\");\n   198→  check_args(c, dilation, padding.size(), \"dilation\");\n   199→\n   200→  // Input\n   201→  checkDimRange(c, input, 3, 6 /* exclusive */);\n   202→  checkSize_symint(c, input, input_channels_dim, weight->size(1) * groups);\n   203→\n   204→  // Weight\n   205→  checkSameDim(c, input, weight);\n   206→\n   207→  // TODO: check that output->size() matches output_sizes\n   208→  // TODO: check that weight matches output->sizes()\n   209→  checkSameDim(c, input, output);\n   210→}\n   211→\n   212→// NB: conv_output_size and conv_input_size are not bijections,\n   213→// as conv_output_size loses information; this is why conv_input_size\n   214→// takes an extra output_padding argument to resolve the ambiguity.\n   215→\n   216→template <typename T>\n   217→inline std::vector<T> _conv_output_size(\n   218→    ArrayRef<T> input_size, ArrayRef<T> weight_size,\n   219→    ArrayRef<T> padding, ArrayRef<T> stride, ArrayRef<T> dilation = ArrayRef<T>()\n   220→) {\n   221→  // ASSERT(input_size.size() > 2)\n   222→  // ASSERT(input_size.size() == weight_size.size())\n   223→  bool has_dilation = !dilation.empty();\n   224→  auto dim = input_size.size();\n   225→  std::vector<T> output_size(dim);\n   226→  output_size[0] = input_size[input_batch_size_dim];\n   227→  output_size[1] = weight_size[weight_output_channels_dim];\n   228→  for (const auto d : c10::irange(2, dim)) {\n   229→    auto dilation_ = has_dilation ? dilation[d - 2] : 1;\n   230→    auto kernel = dilation_ * (weight_size[d] - 1) + 1;\n   231→    output_size[d] = (input_size[d] + (2 * padding[d - 2]) - kernel) / stride[d - 2] + 1;\n   232→  }\n   233→  return output_size;\n   234→}\n   235→\n   236→inline std::vector<int64_t> conv_output_size(\n   237→    IntArrayRef input_size, IntArrayRef weight_size,\n   238→    IntArrayRef padding, IntArrayRef stride, IntArrayRef dilation = IntArrayRef()\n   239→) {\n   240→  return _conv_output_size(input_size, weight_size, padding, stride, dilation);\n   241→}\n   242→\n   243→inline std::vector<c10::SymInt> conv_output_size(\n   244→    SymIntArrayRef input_size, SymIntArrayRef weight_size,\n   245→    SymIntArrayRef padding, SymIntArrayRef stride, SymIntArrayRef dilation = SymIntArrayRef()\n   246→) {\n   247→  return _conv_output_size(input_size, weight_size, padding, stride, dilation);\n   248→}\n   249→\n   250→template <typename T>\n   251→std::vector<T> _conv_input_size(\n   252→    ArrayRef<T> output_size, ArrayRef<T> weight_size,\n   253→    ArrayRef<T> padding, ArrayRef<T> output_padding, ArrayRef<T> stride, ArrayRef<T> dilation, T groups\n   254→) {\n   255→  // ASSERT(output_size.size() > 2)\n   256→  // ASSERT(output_size.size() == weight_size.size())\n   257→  auto dim = output_size.size();\n   258→  std::vector<T> input_size(dim);\n   259→  input_size[0] = output_size[output_batch_size_dim];\n   260→  input_size[1] = weight_size[weight_input_channels_dim] * groups;\n   261→  for (const auto d : c10::irange(2, dim)) {\n   262→ output_padding[d - 2];\n   265→  }\n   266→  return input_size;\n   267→}\n   268→\n   269→inline std::vector<c10::SymInt> conv_input_size(\n   270→    SymIntArrayRef output_size, SymIntArrayRef _conv_input_size(output_size, weight_size, padding, output_padding, stride, dilation, std::move(groups));\n   274→}\n   275→\n   276→inline std::vector<int64_t> conv_input_size(\n   277→ _conv_input_size(output_size, weight_size, padding, output_padding, stride, dilation, groups);\n   281→}\n   282→\n   283→template <typename T>\n   284→std::vector<T> _conv_weight_size(\n   285→    ArrayRef<T> input_size, ArrayRef<T> output_size,\n   286→    ArrayRef<T> padding, ArrayRef<T> output_padding, IntArrayRef stride, IntArrayRef dilation, int64_t groups\n   287→) {\n   288→  auto dim = However, writing a single function that does everything\n// means we get to reuse it for both forwards and all backwards\n// variants, even when the set of \"real\" inputs varies. std::conditional_t<std::is_same_v<param_t, at::Half>, at::opmath_type<param_t>, param_t>;\n  auto dtype = mixed_type ? kFloat : input.scalar_type();\n  if (dtype == kHalf) {\n    dtype = kFloat;\n  }\n\n  auto save_mean_a = save_mean.accessor<param_t, 1>();\n  auto save_var_transform_a = save_var_transform.accessor<param_t, 1>();\n\n  auto running_mean_a = conditional_accessor_1d<param_t>(running_mean);\n  auto running_var_a = conditional_accessor_1d<param_t>(running_var);\n\n  if (all_contiguous) {\n    auto _mean = at::empty({n_input}, input.options().dtype(dtype));\n    auto _var_sum = at::empty({n_input}, input.options().dtype(dtype));\n    auto _mean_a = _mean.accessor<opmath_t, 1>();\n    auto _var_sum_a = _var_sum.accessor<opmath_t, 1>();\n    auto momentum_ = static_cast<opmath_t>(momentum);\n\n    batch_norm_cpu_collect_stats_stub(kCPU, _mean, _var_sum, input);\n\n    parallel_for(0, n_input, 1, [&](int64_t b_begin, int64_t b_end) {\n      for (const auto f : c10::irange(b_begin, b_end)) {\n        save_mean_a[f] = _mean_a[f];\n        save_var_transform_a[f] = VarTransform<accscalar_t>{}(_var_sum_a[f] / n, eps);\n\n        if (running_mean.defined()) {\n          running_mean_a[f] = momentum_ * _mean_a[f] + (1 - momentum_) * running_mean_a[f];\n        }\n        if (running_var.defined()) {\n          accscalar_t unbiased_var = _var_sum_a[f] / (n - 1);\n          running_var_a[f] = momentum_ * unbiased_var + (1 - momentum_) * running_var_a[f];\n        }\n      }\n    });\n\n    return std::make_tuple(save_mean, save_var_transform);\n  }\n\n  // non-contiguous path\n  auto channel_stride = input.strides()[1];\n  auto in_data = input.data_ptr<scalar_t>();\n  auto reduce_iter = TensorIteratorConfig()\n      .add_input(input)\n      .resize_outputs(false)\n      .declare_static_shape(input.sizes(), /*squash_dims=*/1)\n      .check_all_same_dtype(false)\n      .promote_inputs_to_common_dtype(false)\n      .build();\n\n  parallel_for(0, n_input, 1, [&](int64_t b_begin, int64_t b_end) {\n    TensorIterator iter(reduce_iter);\n    for (const auto f : c10::irange(b_begin, b_end)) {\n      // compute variance per input\n      iter.unsafe_replace_operand(0, in_data + channel_stride * f);\n      accscalar_t var_sum = 0;\n      auto mean = static_cast<accscalar_t>(save_mean_a[f]);\n      cpu_serial_kernel(iter, [&](const scalar_t i) -> void {\n        var_sum += (i - mean) * (i - mean);\n      });\n      save_var_transform_a[f] = VarTransform<accscalar_t>{}(var_sum / n, eps);\n\n      // update running averages\n      if (running_mean.defined()) {\n        running_mean_a[f] = momentum * mean + (1 - momentum) * running_mean_a[f];\n      }\n      if (running_var.defined()) {\n        accscalar_t unbiased_var = var_sum / (n - 1);\n        running_var_a[f] = momentum * unbiased_var + (1 - momentum) * running_var_a[f];\n      }\n    }\n  });\n  return std::make_tuple(save_mean, save_var_transform);\n}\n\ntemplate<typename scalar_t, typename param_t, template<typename T> class VarTransform>\nstatic std::tuple<Tensor,Tensor> batch_norm_cpu_update_stats_template(\n    const Tensor& input, const Tensor& running_mean, const Tensor& running_var,\n    double momentum, double eps) {\n  int64_t n_input = input.size(1);\n  const int64_t ndim = input.dim();\n  DimVector reduce_dims(ndim - 1);\n  reduce_dims[0] = 0;\n  for (const auto i : c10::irange(2, ndim)) {\n    reduce_dims[i - 1] = i;\n  }\n\n  constexpr bool mixed_type = !std::is_same_v<scalar_t, param_t>;\n  const auto dtype = mixed_type ? kFloat : input.scalar_type();\n  Tensor save_mean = is_contiguous(input) ? at::empty({n_input}, input.options().dtype(dtype)) : at::mean(input, /*dim=*/reduce_dims, /*keepdim=*/false, dtype);\n  Tensor save_var_transform = at::empty({n_input}, input.options().dtype(dtype));\n  return batch_norm_cpu_update_stats_template<scalar_t, param_t, VarTransform>(input, running_mean, running_var, momentum, eps, save_mean, save_var_transform);\n}\n\ntemplate<typename scalar_t, typename param_t>\nstatic std::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor> batch_norm_backward_cpu_template(\n    const Tensor& grad_out_, const Tensor& input, const Tensor& weight,\n    const Tensor& running_mean, const Tensor& running_var, const Tensor& save_mean, const Tensor& save_invstd,\n    bool train, double eps, std::array<bool,3> grad_input_mask) {\n\n  using accscalar_t = at::acc_type<scalar_t, false>;\n\n  constexpr bool mixed_type = !std::is_same_v<scalar_t, param_t>;\n  const auto dtype = mixed_type ? kFloat : input.scalar_type();\n\n  Tensor grad_input;\n  Tensor grad_weight;\n  Tensor grad_bias;\n  if (grad_input_mask[0]) {\n    grad_input = at::empty_like(input, input.suggest_memory_format());\n  }\n  if (grad_input_mask[1]) {\n    grad_weight = at::empty({input.size(1)}, input.options().dtype(dtype));\n  }\n  if (grad_input_mask[2]) {\n    grad_bias = at::empty({input.size(1)}, input.options().dtype(dtype));\n  }\n\n  // since we are directly manipulating pointers in contiguous path,\n  // need to make sure input and grad_out have the same memory format.\n  bool all_contiguous = is_contiguous(input)\n      && is_contiguous(grad_out_)\n      && input.suggest_memory_format() == grad_out_.suggest_memory_format();\n\n  if (all_contiguous) {\n    if (grad_input_mask[0]) {\n      grad_input = at::empty_like(input, suggest_memory_format_contig(input));\n    }\n    batch_norm_cpu_backward_stub(kCPU, grad_input, grad_weight, grad_bias,\n        grad_out_, input, weight, running_mean, running_var, save_mean, save_invstd, train, eps);\n    return std::make_tuple(grad_input, grad_weight, grad_bias);\n  }\n\n  auto weight_a = conditional_accessor_1d<const param_t>(weight);\n  auto grad_weight_a = conditional_accessor_1d<param_t>(grad_weight);\n  auto grad_bias_a = conditional_accessor_1d<param_t>(grad_bias);\n\n  int64_t n_input = input.size(1);\n  int64_t n = input.numel() / n_input;\n\n  auto save_mean_a = conditional_accessor_1d<const param_t>(save_mean);\n  auto save_invstd_a = conditional_accessor_1d<const param_t>(save_invstd);\n\n  auto running_mean_a = conditional_accessor_1d<const param_t>(running_mean);\n  auto running_var_a = conditional_accessor_1d<const param_t>(running_var);\n\n  const int64_t ndim = input.dim();\n\n  // Reduce all dimensions except dim=1\n  DimVector reduce_dims(ndim - 1);\n  reduce_dims[0] = 0;\n  for (const auto i : c10::irange(2, ndim)) {\n    reduce_dims[i - 1] = i;\n  }\n  // Using float data type for Half sum to avoid overflow\n  // since the representation range of Half is small.\n  auto sum = grad_out_.scalar_type() == kHalf\n      ? at::sum(grad_out_.to(ScalarType::Float), /*dim=*/reduce_dims)\n      : at::sum(grad_out_, /*dim=*/reduce_dims);\n  using sum_t = std::conditional_t<std::is_same_v<scalar_t, at::Half>, float, scalar_t>;\n  auto sum_a = sum.accessor<sum_t, 1>();\n\n  auto reduce_iter = TensorIteratorConfig()\n      .add_const_input(input)\n      .add_const_input(grad_out_)\n      .resize_outputs(false)\n      .declare_static_shape(input.sizes(), /*squash_dims=*/1)\n      .build();\n\n  TensorIterator unary_iter;\n  TensorIterator binary_iter;\n  if (grad_input_mask[0]) {\n    unary_iter.build(\n        TensorIteratorConfig()\n        .add_output(grad_input)\n        .add_const_input(train ? input : grad_out_)\n        .resize_outputs(false)\n        .declare_static_shape(input.sizes(), /*squash_dims=*/1));\n\n    if (train) {\n      binary_iter.build(\n          TensorIteratorConfig()\n          .add_output(grad_input)\n          .add_input(grad_input)\n          .add_const_input(grad_out_)\n          .resize_outputs(false)\n          .declare_static_shape(input.sizes(), /*squash_dims=*/1));\n    }\n  }\n\n  auto in_channel_stride = input.strides()[1];\n  auto in_data = input.const_data_ptr<scalar_t>();\n  auto grad_in_channel_stride = grad_input_mask[0] ? grad_input.strides()[1] : 0;\n  auto grad_in_data = grad_input_mask[0] ? grad_input.mutable_data_ptr<scalar_t>() : nullptr;\n  auto grad_out_channel_stride = grad_out_.strides()[1];\n  auto grad_out_data = grad_out_.const_data_ptr<scalar_t>();\n\n  parallel_for(0, n_input, 1, [&](int64_t b_begin, int64_t b_end) {\n      TensorIterator reduce_iter_local(reduce_iter);\n      TensorIterator unary_iter_local(unary_iter);\n      TensorIterator binary_iter_local(binary_iter);\n\n      for (const auto f : c10::irange(b_begin, b_end)) {\n        param_t w = weight.defined() ? weight_a[f] : param_t(1);\n\n        param_t mean{}, invstd{};\n        if (train) {\n          mean = save_mean_a[f];\n          invstd = save_invstd_a[f];\n        } else {\n          mean = running_mean_a[f];\n          invstd = 1 / std::sqrt(running_var_a[f] + eps);\n        }\n\n        // dot product of the Q(X) and gradOutput\n        accscalar_t dotp = 0;\n        reduce_iter_local.unsafe_replace_operand(\n            0, const_cast<scalar_t*>(in_data + f * in_channel_stride));\n        reduce_iter_local.unsafe_replace_operand(\n            1, const_cast<scalar_t*>(grad_out_data + f * grad_out_channel_stride));\n\n        cpu_serial_kernel(reduce_iter_local, [&](const scalar_t i, const scalar_t go) -> void {\n          dotp += (i - mean) * go;\n        });\n\n        if (grad_input_mask[0]) {\n          if (train) {\n            // when in training mode\n            // Q(X) = X - E[x] ; i.e. input centered to zero mean\n            // Y = Q(X) / sigma    ; i.e. BN output before weight and bias\n            // dL/dX = (Q(dL/dY) - dot(Y, dL/dY) * Y) / sigma * w\n\n            // projection of gradOutput on to output scaled by std\n            scalar_t k = (scalar_t) dotp * invstd * invstd / n;\n            {\n              unary_iter_local.unsafe_replace_operand(\n                  0, grad_in_data + f * grad_in_channel_stride);\n              unary_iter_local.unsafe_replace_operand(\n                  1, const_cast<scalar_t*>(in_data + f * in_channel_stride));\n              cpu_serial_kernel(unary_iter_local, [&](const scalar_t i) -> scalar_t {\n                return (i - mean) * k;\n              });\n            }\n\n            scalar_t grad_mean = sum_a[f] / n;\n            {\n              auto gI_data = grad_in_data + f * grad_in_channel_stride;\n              binary_iter_local.unsafe_replace_operand(0, gI_data);\n              binary_iter_local.unsafe_replace_operand(1, gI_data);\n              binary_iter_local.unsafe_replace_operand(\n                  2, const_cast<scalar_t*>(grad_out_data + f * grad_out_channel_stride));\n              cpu_serial_kernel(binary_iter_local, [&](scalar_t gi, scalar_t go) -> scalar_t {\n                return (go - grad_mean - gi) * invstd * w;\n              });\n            }\n          } else {\n            // when in evaluation mode\n            // Q(X) = X - running_mean  ; i.e. input centered to zero mean\n            // Y = Q(X) / running_std    ; i.e. BN output before weight and bias\n            // dL/dX = w / running_std\n            {\n              unary_iter_local.unsafe_replace_operand(\n                  0, grad_in_data + f * grad_in_channel_stride);\n              unary_iter_local.unsafe_replace_operand(\n                  1, const_cast<scalar_t*>(grad_out_data + f * grad_out_channel_stride));\n              cpu_serial_kernel(unary_iter_local, [&](const scalar_t i) -> scalar_t {\n                return i * invstd * w;\n              });\n            }\n          }\n        }\n        if (grad_input_mask[1]) {\n          grad_weight_a[f] = dotp * invstd;\n        }\n\n        if (grad_input_mask[2]) {\n          grad_bias_a[f] = sum_a[f];\n        }\n      }\n    });\n  return std::make_tuple(grad_input, grad_weight, grad_bias);\n}\n\nBatchNormBackend _select_batch_norm_backend(\n    const Tensor& input, const Tensor& weight, const Tensor& bias, const Tensor& running_mean,\n    const Tensor& running_var, bool training, double eps) {\n\n  auto& ctx = at::globalContext();\n  bool cudnn_enabled = ctx.userEnabledCuDNN();\n\n  if (\n      input.is_cuda()\n      && input.scalar_type() != at::kBFloat16 && weight.scalar_type() != at::kBFloat16\n      && (input.scalar_type() != at::kHalf\n        || weight.scalar_type() == at::kFloat)\n      && weight.defined() && bias.defined()\n      && ((running_mean.defined() && running_var.defined())\n        || (!running_mean.defined() && !running_var.defined() && training))\n      && (input.dim() >= 3)\n      && ((input.sym_size(0) <= 880801 && training) // spatial, training\n          ||(input.sym_size(0) <= 65535 && !training)) //spatial, eval\n      && detail::getCUDAHooks().compiledWithCuDNN()\n      && eps >= detail::getCUDAHooks().batchnormMinEpsilonCuDNN()\n      && cudnn_enabled && detail::getCUDAHooks().versionCuDNN() >= 5110L\n      && input.sym_numel() < std::numeric_limits<std::int32_t>::max() // some cuDNN kernels have 32-bit indexing limitations\n  ) {\n    return BatchNormBackend::Cudnn;\n  }\n\n  // TODO: Remove PYTORCH_MIOPEN_SUGGEST_NHWC_BATCHNORM once ROCm officially supports NHWC in MIOpen\n  // See https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/64427.\n  // non static variable is used to be able to change environment variable in runtime for testing\n  // enabled by default for ROCm >= 7.0.0 with miopen 3.5\n  int miopen_version = detail::getCUDAHooks().compiledWithMIOpen() ? detail::getCUDAHooks().versionMIOpen() : 0;\n  bool is_miopen_3_4 = miopen_version >= 30400;  // ROCm 6.4\n  bool is_miopen_3_5 = miopen_version >= 30500;  // ROCm 7.0\n  bool PYTORCH_MIOPEN_SUGGEST_NHWC_BATCHNORM = c10::utils::check_env(\"PYTORCH_MIOPEN_SUGGEST_NHWC_BATCHNORM\").value_or(is_miopen_3_5);\n\n  if (\n      detail::getCUDAHooks().compiledWithMIOpen()\n      && cudnn_enabled\n      && input.is_cuda()\n      && input.dim() <= MIOPEN_DIM_MAX\n      && input.dim() >= 3\n      && input.scalar_type() != at::kDouble\n      && (is_miopen_3_4 || input.scalar_type() != at::kBFloat16)\n      && weight.scalar_type() == at::kFloat // only FP32 weight for FP32 or FP16/BF16(mixed) input\n      && weight.defined() && bias.defined()\n      && ((running_mean.defined() && running_var.defined())\n        || (!running_mean.defined() && !running_var.defined() && training))\n      && (input.suggest_memory_format() == MemoryFormat::Contiguous\n          || (is_miopen_3_5 && PYTORCH_MIOPEN_SUGGEST_NHWC_BATCHNORM &&\n              (input.suggest_memory_format() == MemoryFormat::ChannelsLast\n               || input.suggest_memory_format() == MemoryFormat::ChannelsLast3d)))\n  ) {\n    return BatchNormBackend::Miopen;\n  }\n\n  return BatchNormBackend::Native;\n}\n\n\n// _batch_norm_impl_index(_backward) are used in the JIT be able to keep the run-time selection\n// of backends, while enabling it to keep the information about the used backend, so that it can\n// use its corresponding backward implementation.\n// XXX: The indices of backends need to be kept synchronized between this function and its _backward.\n// TODO: remove cudnn_enabled arg\nstd::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, int64_t> _batch_norm_impl_index(\n    const Tensor& input, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& bias_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_mean_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_var_opt /* optional */,\n    bool training, double momentum, double eps, bool cudnn_enabled) {\n  // See [Note: hacky wrapper removal for optional tensor]\n  c10::MaybeOwned<Tensor> weight_maybe_owned = at::borrow_from_optional_tensor(weight_opt);\n  const Tensor& weight = *weight_maybe_owned;\n  const Tensor& bias = bias_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_mean = running_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_var = running_var_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n\n  auto num_features = input.sym_sizes()[1];\n\n  if (input.sym_numel() == 0) {\n    Tensor reserve = at::empty({0}, input.options().dtype(kByte));\n    auto options = input.options().dtype(\n        at::toAccumulateType(input.scalar_type(), input.device().type()));\n    auto save_mean = at::empty_symint(c10::SymIntArrayRef({num_features}), options);\n    auto save_invstd = at::empty_symint(c10::SymIntArrayRef({std::move(num_features)}), options);\n\n    // don't return view of input, don't return empty tensor because it will break gradient chain\n    auto out = input.clone();\n    if (weight.defined()) out = out * weight[0];\n    if (bias.defined()) out = out + bias[0];\n    return std::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, int64_t>(\n        out, save_mean, save_invstd, reserve, 0);\n  }\n\n  if (running_mean.defined()) {\n    check_dims_match_num_input_features(\"running_mean\", num_features, running_mean.sym_numel());\n  } else if (!training) {\n    TORCH_CHECK(false, \"running_mean must be defined in evaluation mode\");\n  }\n  if (running_var.defined()) {\n    check_dims_match_num_input_features(\"running_var\", num_features, running_var.sym_numel());\n  } else if (!training) {\n    TORCH_CHECK(false, \"running_var must be defined in evaluation mode\");\n  }\n  if (weight.defined()) {\n    check_dims_match_num_input_features(\"weight\", num_features, weight.sym_numel());\n  }\n  if (bias.defined()) {\n    check_dims_match_num_input_features(\"bias\", std::move(num_features), bias.sym_numel());\n  }\n\n  BatchNormBackend backend = _select_batch_norm_backend(input, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var, training, eps);\n\n  if (backend == BatchNormBackend::Cudnn) {\n    auto input_c = input.contiguous(input.suggest_memory_format());\n    auto weight_c = weight.contiguous();\n    auto bias_c = bias.contiguous();\n    auto rmean_c = running_mean.defined() ? running_mean.contiguous() : running_mean;\n    auto rvar_c = running_var.defined() ? running_var.contiguous() : running_var;\n\n    auto [output, save_mean, save_var, reserve] =\n        at::cudnn_batch_norm(input_c, weight_c, bias_c, rmean_c, rvar_c,\n                             training, momentum, eps);\n\n    return std::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, int64_t>(\n        output, save_mean, save_var, reserve, 1);\n  }\n\n  Tensor reserve = at::empty({0}, input.options().dtype(kByte));\n\n  if (backend == BatchNormBackend::Miopen) {\n    return std::tuple_cat(\n             at::miopen_batch_norm(\n               input.contiguous(), weight.contiguous(), bias.contiguous(),\n               running_mean.defined() ? running_mean.contiguous() : running_mean,\n               running_var.defined() ? running_var.contiguous() : running_var,\n               training, momentum, eps),\n             std::tuple<Tensor>(reserve),\n             std::make_tuple(2));\n  }\n\n  return std::tuple_cat(\n           at::native_batch_norm(\n             input, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var, training, momentum, eps),\n           std::tuple<Tensor>(reserve),\n           std::make_tuple(0));\n}\n\nstd::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor> _batch_norm_impl_index_backward(\n    int64_t impl_index,\n    const Tensor& input, const Tensor& grad_output, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_mean_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_var_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& save_mean_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& save_var_transform_opt /* optional */,\n    bool train, double epsilon, std::array<bool, 3> output_mask, const Tensor &reservedSpace) {\n  // See [Note: hacky wrapper removal for optional tensor]\n  c10::MaybeOwned<Tensor> weight_maybe_owned = at::borrow_from_optional_tensor(weight_opt);\n  const Tensor& weight = *weight_maybe_owned;\n  const Tensor& running_mean = running_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_var = running_var_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& save_mean = save_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& save_var_transform = save_var_transform_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n\n  if (input.numel() == 0) {\n    std::vector<int64_t> dims(input.dim() - 1);\n    dims[0] = 0;\n    std::iota(dims.begin() + 1, dims.end(), 2);\n\n    // don't return empty tensor because it will break gradient chain\n    Tensor grad_input;\n    Tensor grad_weight;\n    Tensor grad_bias;\n    if (output_mask[2]) {\n      grad_bias = grad_output.sum(dims);\n    }\n    if (output_mask[1]) {\n      grad_weight = (grad_output * input).sum(dims);\n    }\n    if (output_mask[0] && weight.defined()) {\n      grad_input = grad_output * weight[0];\n    }\n    return std::make_tuple(grad_input, grad_weight, grad_bias);\n  }\n\n  // backward in inference mode is not supported in cudnn, fallback to native\n  if (impl_index == 0 || (!train)) {\n    return at::native_batch_norm_backward(grad_output, input, weight, running_mean, running_var, save_mean, save_var_transform, train, epsilon, output_mask);\n  } else if (impl_index == 1) {\n    // TODO: _batch_norm_impl_index_backward is only used in JIT. cudnn NHWC\n    // format conversion is done inside cudnn_batch_norm_backward instead\n    return at::cudnn_batch_norm_backward(input, grad_output, weight, running_mean, running_var, save_mean, save_var_transform, epsilon, reservedSpace);\n  } else if (impl_index == 2) {\n    return at::miopen_batch_norm_backward(input, grad_output, weight, running_mean, running_var, save_mean, save_var_transform, epsilon);\n  }\n  TORCH_INTERNAL_ASSERT(false, \"Unsupported impl_index in _batch_norm_impl_index_backward: \", impl_index);\n}\n\n// TODO: remove cudnn_enabled arg\nTensor batch_norm(\n    const Tensor& input, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& bias_opt,\n    const std::optional<Tensor>& running_mean_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_var_opt,\n    bool training, double momentum, double eps, bool cudnn_enabled) {\n  const Tensor& weight = weight_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& bias = bias_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_mean = running_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_var = running_var_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  return std::get<0>(at::_batch_norm_impl_index(input, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var,\n                                                training, momentum, eps, cudnn_enabled));\n  // TODO: switch to the new stack after the 2 week FC window\n  // if (training) {\n  //   BatchNormBackend backend = _select_batch_norm_backend(input, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var, training, eps);\n  //   if (backend == BatchNormBackend::Cudnn || backend == BatchNormBackend::Miopen) {\n  //     auto input_c = input;\n  //     if (backend == BatchNormBackend::Cudnn) {\n  //         input_c = input.contiguous(input.suggest_memory_format());\n  //     } else {\n  //         input_c = input.contiguous();\n  //     }\n  //     auto weight_c = weight.contiguous();\n  //     auto bias_c = bias.contiguous();\n  //     auto rmean_c = running_mean.defined() ? running_mean.contiguous() : running_mean;\n  //     auto rvar_c = running_var.defined() ? running_var.contiguous() : running_var;\n  //     return std::get<0>(at::_batch_norm_with_update(input_c, weight_c, bias_c, const_cast<Tensor&>(rmean_c),\n  //                                                   const_cast<Tensor&>(rvar_c), momentum, eps));\n  //   } else {\n  //     return std::get<0>(at::_batch_norm_with_update(input, weight, bias, const_cast<Tensor&>(running_mean),\n  // eps, bool cudnn_enabled) {\n  // See [Note: hacky wrapper removal for optional tensor]\n  c10::MaybeOwned<Tensor> weight_maybe_owned = at::borrow_from_optional_tensor(weight_opt);\n  const Tensor& If any filter fails, then use_<backend> returns false.\n*\n* In order to aid in debugging, each filter takes sdp_params and a debug flag.\n* If the debug flag is set, the filter will print a warning message if it fails.\n* The behavior of select_sdp_backend is to return the first backend that\n* succeeds. The use_<backend> function\n* will iterate over a list of \"filters\" that check for specific properties of\n* the SDP parameters. If all filters pass, the backend can be used and use_<backend>\n* returns true. If any filter fails, then use_<backend> returns false.\n*\n* In order to aid in debugging, each filter takes sdp_params and a debug flag.\n* If the debug flag is set, the filter will print a warning message if it fails.\n* The behavior of select_sdp_backend is to return the first backend that\n* succeeds. If no backend is viable then it will run each use_<backend> function\n* with debug=true and return SDPBackend::error.\n*/\n\nnamespace sdp {\nnamespace {\n\n// tracks whether we've set the default priority order once, to avoid setting\n// it redundantly or overwriting a user-specified priority order\n// when the priority order context manager is used before the default priority\n// order is initialized the following happens:\n// (1) the current priority order is queried\n// (2) priority_order() is called, which initializes it to the default as init_ is false\n// (3) the user-specified priority order is set\n// (3.1) we are in the priority context...\n// (3.2) we exit the priority context...\n// (4) the previous priority order (default) is restored\nbool priority_order_init_ = false;\n\n// TODO(eqy): more benchmarking to determine whether this should include sm86/89\n// Needs to be kept in-sync with test_fused_chocie in test_transformers.py\nbool check_prefer_cudnn_attention() {\n  static const bool prefer_cudnn = c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_PREFERRED\") != false;\n  if (!prefer_cudnn) {\n    return false;\n  }\n#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION)\n  long cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();\n  if (cudnn_version >= 90900) {\n    auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n    auto major = dprops->major;\n    return (major == 9 || major == 10) && !dprops->minor;\n  }\n#endif\n  return false;\n}\n\n// flash_attention V2 is universally faster than efficient_attention and Math\nstd::array<SDPBackend, num_backends> priority_order(sdp_params const& params) {\n  if (!priority_order_init_) {\n    priority_order_init_ = true;\n    if (check_prefer_cudnn_attention()) {\n        const std::vector<int64_t> cudnn_order = {static_cast<int64_t>(at::SDPBackend::cudnn_attention),\n                                                  static_cast<int64_t>(at::SDPBackend::flash_attention),\n                                                  static_cast<int64_t>(at::SDPBackend::efficient_attention),\n                                                  static_cast<int64_t>(at::SDPBackend::math)};\n        at::globalContext().setSDPPriorityOrder(cudnn_order);\n    }\n  }\n  return at::globalContext().sDPPriorityOrder();\n}\n\nbool use_tensor_cores(sdp_params const& params, cudaDeviceProp* dprops, bool is_half) {\n  if (dprops->major >= 8) {\n    return true;\n  }\n  if (dprops->major >= 7) {\n    return is_half;\n  }\n  return false;\n}\nint64_t minimum_gemm_alignment(sdp_params const& params) {\n  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n  bool is_half = (params.query.dtype() == at::kHalf) ||\n      (params.query.dtype() == at::kBFloat16);\n  bool use_tc = use_tensor_cores(params, dprops, is_half);\n  int64_t matmul_alignment_mn = 1;\n  if (dprops->major >= 8) {\n    matmul_alignment_mn = 4;\n check_requires_grad_and_head_dim_gt192_constraints_on_sm86_89_or_120(\n    sdp_params const& params,\n    bool debug) {\n  // Flash Attention will raise an error in the backward pass if the head_dim\n (debug) {\n    TORCH_WARN(CUDNN_VERSION, \" cuDNN version too old to use cuDNN Attention (< v9.0.0)\");\n  }\n  return false;\n#endif\n#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION)\n  static auto cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();\n  if (params.dropout > 0.0 && cudnn_version > 91100 && cudnn_version < 91400) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(CUDNN_VERSION, \" cuDNN version          check_all_tensors_on_device,\n          check_tensor_shapes,\n          check_cudnn_deterministic,\n          check_dtypes_low_precision,\n          check_attn_mask_shape,\n          check_cudnn_hardware_support\n          );\n  for (auto& constraint : general_constraints) {\n    if (!constraint(params, debug)) {\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n  constexpr auto dense_constraints =\n      c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(\n      check_nonzero_sequence_lengths_dense,\n      check_last_dim_stride_equals_1_dense<true /*ignore_singleton_dim=*/>,\n      check_batch_size_and_num_heads_dense<true /*enable_gqa*/, false /*requires_same_num_heads*/>,\n      check_cudnn_tensor_shapes\n  );\n\n  if (has_only_dense_inputs(params)) {\n    for (auto& constraint : dense_constraints) {\n      if (!constraint(params, debug)) {\n        return false;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool is_flash_attention_available() {\n#ifdef USE_FLASH_ATTENTION\n  return true;\n#else\n  return false;\n#endif\n}\n\nbool can_use_flash_attention(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n#ifndef USE_FLASH_ATTENTION\n  if (debug) {\n    TORCH_WARN(\"Torch was not compiled with flash attention.\");\n  }\n  return false;\n#else // defined(USE_FLASH_ATTENTION)\n  // Define gate functions that determine if a flash kernel can be ran\n  // nested_constraints) {\n      if (!constraint(params, debug)) {\n        return false;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  constexpr bool backend_supports_grouped_query_attention = true;\n  if check_batch_size_and_num_heads_dense<backend_supports_grouped_query_attention>,\n        check_nonzero_sequence_lengths_dense,\n        check_last_dim_stride_equals_1_dense<true defined(USE_FLASH_ATTENTION)\n}\n\nbool can_use_mem_efficient_attention(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n#ifndef USE_MEM_EFF_ATTENTION\n  TORCH_WARN_ONCE(!debug, \"Torch was not compiled with memory efficient attention.\");\n  return false;\n#endif\n  // Constraints specific to mem efficient attention\n  constexpr auto less_than_sm80_mem_efficient_dtypes =\n      c10::array_of<at::ScalarType>(at::kHalf, at::kFloat);\n#ifdef USE_ROCM\n  constexpr auto aotriton_mem_efficient_dtypes =\n      c10::array_of<at::ScalarType>(at::kHalf, at::kFloat, at::kBFloat16);\n  constexpr auto ck_mem_efficient_dtypes =\n      c10::array_of<at::ScalarType>(at::kHalf, at::kBFloat16);\n#else\n  constexpr auto greater_than_or_equal_sm80_mem_efficient_dtypes =\n      c10::array_of<at::ScalarType>(at::kHalf, at::kFloat, at::kBFloat16);\n#endif\n\n  //  Define gate functions that determine if a mem efficient kernel can be ran\n  constexpr auto general_constraints = c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(\n      check_runtime_disabled_mem_efficient,\n      check_all_tensors_on_device,\n      check_mem_efficient_hardware_support,\n      check_tensor_shapes,\n#ifdef USE_ROCM\n      check_head_dim_size_flash<true /* caller_is_meff */>\n#else\n      check_head_dim_size_mem_efficient\n#endif\n  );\n  for (auto& constraint : (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(\n#ifndef USE_ROCM  // ME and FA shares backend on ROCM and thus supports training\n        check_requires_grad_and_nested,\n#else // Meanwhile ME on ROCM share the greater_than_or_equal_sm80_mem_efficient_dtypes, debug);\n  }\n#endif\n  return check_tensor_dtype(params, less_than_sm80_mem_efficient_dtypes, debug);\n}\n\nSDPBackend select_sdp_backend(sdp_params const& kernel_params) {\n  // This function defines the priority order of the different sdp backends\n  // 1. Flash Attention\n  // 2. Mem Efficient Attention\n  // 3. Math fallback\n  auto& ctx = at::globalContext();\n  if (!ctx.userEnabledMathSDP() && !ctx.userEnabledFlashSDP() &&\n      !ctx.userEnabledMemEfficientSDP() && !ctx.userEnabledCuDNNSDP()) {\n    return SDPBackend::error;\n  }\n  // Get ideal kernel ordering\n  const auto ordering = priority_order(kernel_params);\n\n  // Because TORCHCHECK checks if condition is true we negate debug so that\n  // The statements will be printed when debug is true\n  bool print_debug = false;\n  for (auto& backend : ordering) {\n    switch (backend) {\n      case SDPBackend::cudnn_attention:\n        if (sdp::can_use_cudnn_attention(kernel_params, print_debug)) {\n              return SDPBackend::cudnn_attention;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::flash_attention:\n        if (sdp::can_use_flash_attention(kernel_params, print_debug)) {\n          return SDPBackend::flash_attention;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::efficient_attention:\n        if (sdp::can_use_mem_efficient_attention(kernel_params, print_debug)) {\n          return SDPBackend::efficient_attention;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::math:\n        if (ctx.userEnabledMathSDP()) {\n          return SDPBackend::math;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::overrideable:\n        if (ctx.userEnabledOverrideableSDP()) {\n          TORCH_CHECK(false, \"Invalid backend\");\n        }\n        break;\n      default:\n        TORCH_CHECK(false, \"Invalid backend\");\n    }\n  }\n  // If we have gotten to this point then two things have happened:\n  // 1. use_flash_attention or use_mem_efficient did not satisfy the\n  // constraints to be ran\n  // 2. The user has explicitly disabled the math kernel\n  // We then re-run the kernel checks with debug enabled to print out the\n  // reason why the kernel was not selected\n\n  print_debug = true;\n  TORCH_WARN(\"Memory efficient kernel not used because:\");\n  sdp::can_use_mem_efficient_attention(kernel_params, print_debug);\n  TORCH_WARN(\"Flash attention kernel not used because:\");\n  sdp::can_use_flash_attention(kernel_params, print_debug);\n  TORCH_WARN(\"cuDNN attention kernel not used because:\");\n  sdp::can_use_cudnn_attention(kernel_params, print_debug);\n  TORCH_CHECK(!print_debug, \"No available kernel. Aborting execution.\")\n  return SDPBackend::error;\n}\n\nbool check_for_seq_len_1_nested_tensor(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  // When this function is called we are assured that the nt is dim==4\n  if (!params.query.is_nested()) {\n    return true;\n  }\n\n  const auto nt_q_tensor_impl =\n      at::native::get_nested_tensor_impl(params.query);\n  const at::Tensor& sizes = nt_q_tensor_impl->get_nested_sizes();\n  auto* sizes_ptr = sizes.data_ptr<int64_t>();\n  const int64_t n_tensors = params.query.size(0);\n  const int64_t size_tensor_stride = sizes.stride(0);\n\n  // This is being called inside sdp with shape [batch, heads, {seq_len}, dim]\n  for (const auto i : c10::irange(n_tensors)) {\n    if (sizes_ptr[(i * size_tensor_stride) + 1] <= 1) {\n      if (debug) {\n        TORCH_WARN(\n            \"Packed projection for fused kernels does not support sequence_length <= 1\");\n      }\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return true;\n}\n\n} // namespace sdp\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":663,"oldLines":17,"newStart":663,"newLines":17,"lines":["   }","   return false;"," #endif","-#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && CUDNN_VERSION < 90000","-  if (debug) {","-    TORCH_WARN(CUDNN_VERSION, \" cuDNN version too old to use cuDNN Attention (< v9.0.0)\");","-  }","-  return false;","-#endif"," #if defined(CUDNN_VERSION)","   static auto cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();","+  if (cudnn_version < 90000) {","+    if (debug) {","+      TORCH_WARN(cudnn_version, \" cuDNN version too old to use cuDNN Attention (< v9.0.0)\");","+    }","+    return false;","+  }","   if (params.dropout > 0.0 && cudnn_version > 91100 && cudnn_version < 91400) {","     if (debug) {","-      TORCH_WARN(CUDNN_VERSION, \" cuDNN version does not support droppout in SDPA (9.11 -
